## blessonism/openclaw-memory-architecture

> [!info]
> вӯҗ 16 В· JavaScript В· 2026-02-24  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/blessonism/openclaw-memory-architecture)  
> `#AI жҷәиғҪдҪ“` `#Memory System` `#Two-Layer Architecture` 
> OpenClaw Memory Architecture is a battle-tested two-layer memory system for AI agents requiring cross-session persistence. It features a hot cache (MEMORY.md) and deep storage (memory/), deterministic lookup paths, embedding-based semantic search, a program clerk for knowledge curation, and a Supersede mechanism for fact evolution tracking, all built on transparent, Git-friendly file storage.
> <sub>A battle-tested two-layer memory system for AI agents that need to remember across sessions.</sub>

> [GitHub](https://github.com/yuanfengyun/mj_ai)  
> `#KNN Algorithm` `#Mahjong AI` `#Probability Estimation` 
> This repository implements a Mahjong AI algorithm using multiple approaches: full probability estimation, local probability estimation, and deep learning. It employs KNN to match melded hands and calculates winning probabilities for optimal tile discard. Supports 14-tile hands of Wan-Tong-Tiao suits, with C version (6s) significantly faster than Lua (900s). Future work includes suit-based probability aggregation and honor tile handling.
> <sub>йә»е°ҶAIз®—жі•пјҲеҢ…еҗ«е…ЁжҰӮзҺҮдј°з®—гҖҒеұҖйғЁжҰӮзҺҮдј°з®—гҖҒж·ұеәҰеӯҰд№ зүҲжң¬пјү</sub>
